#Divers
company_BasicBank = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/bank/BasicBank.dds" 
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_manufactering_light.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	replaces_company = company_basic_bank
	 
	uses_dynamic_naming = yes

	dynamic_company_type_names = {
		"dynamic_company_type_company"
		"dynamic_company_type_consortium"
		"dynamic_company_type_corporation" 
	}


	building_types = {  
		building_ef_private_construction
		building_railway
		building_port
		building_trade_center
		building_gold_mine
		building_silver_mine

		building_financial_centre
	} 

	potential = { 
		has_modifier = has_central_bank
		not = {  
			OR = {  
				c:USA ?= this
				c:NET ?= this
				c:BEL ?= this
				c:SWI ?= this
				c:SWE ?= this
				c:DEN ?= this
				c:NOR ?= this
				c:SPA ?= this
				c:POR ?= this
				c:ITA ?= this
				c:SAR ?= this
				c:SIC ?= this
				c:GBR ?= this
				c:FRA ?= this
				c:RUS ?= this
				c:PRU ?= this
				c:GER ?= this
				c:FRM ?= this
				c:BAV ?= this
				c:AUS ?= this
				c:GRE ?= this
				c:TUR ?= this
				c:PER ?= this
				c:EGY ?= this
				c:CHI ?= this
				c:JAP ?= this
				c:BIC ?= this
				c:CAN ?= this
				c:QUE ?= this
				c:ONT ?= this
				c:COS ?= this
				c:MEX ?= this
				c:HON ?= this
				c:PNM ?= this
				c:BRZ ?= this
				c:ARG ?= this
				c:CHL ?= this
				c:BOL ?= this
				c:CLM ?= this
				c:VNZ ?= this
				c:CUB ?= this
				c:URU ?= this
				c:PRG ?= this
				c:SAF ?= this 
			}
		}
	}

	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_financial_district
				level >= 1
			}
		}
	}

	prosperity_modifier = { 
		country_minting_mult = 0.075  
		building_group_bg_heavy_industry_throughput_add = 0.05 #invested a lot in heavy industries, steel railways, war...

		country_loan_interest_rate_mult = -0.05
        country_private_construction_allocation_mult = 0.05

		state_farmers_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.01
		state_shopkeepers_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.01
		state_clergymen_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.04
		state_aristocrats_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.04
		state_capitalists_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.065

		building_nationalization_investment_return_add = 0.05
		country_government_dividends_reinvestment_add = 0.05
		country_government_dividends_efficiency_add = 0.05

		country_max_companies_add = 1
	}
	 
	ai_will_do = {
		always = yes
	}

	ai_construction_targets = {
		any_scope_state = {
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_ef_private_construction
				level >= 5
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

	preferred_headquarters = {STATE_BAJO_PARAGUAY }

	building_types = {
		building_ef_private_construction
		building_railway
		building_port
		building_trade_center
		building_gold_mine
		building_silver_mine

		building_financial_centre
	}

	potential = {
		country_has_primary_culture = cu:platinean
	}

	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_financial_district
				level >= 1
			}
		}
	}

	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BAJO_PARAGUAY # Asuncion
			}
		}
	}

	prosperity_modifier = {
		building_cash_reserves_mult = 0.05

		country_loan_interest_rate_mult = -0.05
		country_private_construction_allocation_mult = 0.05

		state_farmers_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.015
		state_shopkeepers_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.015
		state_clergymen_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.04
		state_aristocrats_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.04
		state_capitalists_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.065

		building_nationalization_investment_return_add = 0.05
		country_government_dividends_reinvestment_add = 0.075
		country_government_dividends_efficiency_add = 0.075

		country_max_companies_add = 1
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		always = yes
	}
}

	}

		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_southern_africa
	}

	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				OR = {
					state_region = s:STATE_EASTERN_CAPE
					state_region = s:STATE_CAPE_COLONY
				}
			}
		}
	}

	possible = {

				is_building_type = building_financial_district
				level >= 1
			}
		}
	}

		building_gold_mine_throughput_add = 0.15 #involved in diamond/gold trade

		state_shopkeepers_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.04
		state_clergymen_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.04
		state_aristocrats_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.04
		state_capitalists_investment_pool_contribution_add = 0.065

		building_nationalization_investment_return_add = 0.05
		country_government_dividends_reinvestment_add = 0.05

	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_oil_drills.dds"

	replaces_company = company_standard_oil

	building_types = {
		building_oil_rig
		building_railway
		building_ef_private_construction
	}

	extension_building_types = {
		building_port
	}

	possible_prestige_goods = {
		mining_stock_usa
		prestige_good_usa_oil
	}

	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_the_midwest
	}

	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				region = sr:region_the_midwest
			}
		}
	}

	possible = {
		has_technology_researched = pumpjacks
		any_scope_state = {
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_oil_rig
				#level >= 5
			}
		}
	}

	prosperity_modifier = {
		building_railway_throughput_add = 0.2
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		has_technology_researched = pumpjacks
		any_scope_state = {
			is_incorporated = yes
			has_potential_resource = bg_oil_extraction
		}
	}

	ai_construction_targets = {
		building_oil_rig = {
			level = 5
			state_trigger = {
				region = sr:region_the_midwest
				is_incorporated = yes
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		value = 50 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}
